From the kitchen of Terri Board

Sweet potato casserole with a pecan streusel topping sits at the intersection of Southern and Midwestern holiday cooking a dish that crossed the Mason-Dixon line and became a fixture at Thanksgiving tables throughout Ohio. For NE Ohio families, it represented the kind of abundant, sweet-savory side dish that made holiday meals feel genuinely special.
